 But it is not that you cannot avoid it

 Here are some tips that you can protect yourself in office politics
 1
 Accept - If you are being drawn into politics, then you first accept that situation
 uske baad aap uske asli kaarnon ko khojna shuru karen
 After this you have options to give, either you accept the situation and let it go or fight against it
 2
 Do not favor anyone - when we start favoring someone, we get into trouble
 kisi maamle par apana vichaar rakhana sahi hota he lekin kisi kaa paksh lenaa sahi nahin he
 You should not fall into a disagreement between two people and do evil to another
 3
 Don't be personal with anyone - if the person who works with you in the office fights with you then there is no need to take revenge from him
 agar aap bhi uske saath ladaai main padate hai to aapaki image aapkeboske saamne kharaab ho jaaegi

 Don't send an angry mail - think a hundred times before sending any
 ho saktaa he gusse main aap mail main kuch bhi likh den lekin aage chalakar isse aapaki image kharaab ho sakati he

 Keep the identity of the real criminal - you should know that who is guilty and should always try to stay away from him

 The Yogi government is bringing UPCOCA along the lines of MCOCA to clamp down on criminals in Uttar Pradesh
 ye vidheyak mangalvaar ko upi vidhansabha main paarit ho gaya
 Under this new strict law, crimes like underworld, extortion, forcible houses and land capture, prostitution, kidnapping, ransom, intimidation, trafficking will be included
 bharat main maharashtra ke baad uttar pradesh doosraa aisa doosraa pradesh he, jahaan itnaa sakht kanoon lagu kiya jane kii taiyaari chal rahi he
 upkokayani Uttar Pradesh Control of Organized Crime Act has the following provisions - Any person committing organized crime of any kind will fall under this law
 - is kanoon ke tahat giraftaar vyakti ko 6 maheene tak jamaanat nahin milegi
 Under this law, a case will be registered only if the accused has been involved in at least two organized crimes
 uske khilaaf chargeshit daakhil kii gai ho
 - You will get 180 days to file a charge sheet against the culprit arrested in UPCOCA
 abhi tak ke kanoonon main 60 se 90 din hi milte hai
 Under UPCOCA, the police can take the remand of the accused for 30 days, while the rest of the laws only get 15 days remand
 - is kanoon ke tahat kam se kam apradhi ko paanch saal kii sajaa mil sakati he
 There will be a provision for maximum hanging
 itane sakht kanoon kaa durupyog naa ho, ye tay karne ke liye upicoca ke maamalon main cese darj karne or jaanch karne ke liye bhi alag niyam banaaye gaye hai
 - The Home Secretary will monitor such cases at the state level
 - mandal ke str par aiji rank ke adhikari kii sanstuti ke baad hi cese darj kiya jayega
 - If at the district level there is an organized crime taker, then the commissioner, DM will report it
 - upicoca sangathit aparaadh ke khilaaf police ko bahut se adhikaar detaa he
 Under Section 28 (3A) of UPCOCA, the police can keep an accused in lock-up for 60 days without even being proved guilty
 - ipisi kii dhaaraon ke tahat giraftaar ke 60 se 90 dinon ke andar chargeshit daakhil kerani hoti he, vahiin upicoca main 180 dinon tak bina chargeshit daakhil kiye aaropee ko jail main rakhaa ja sakegaa
 - This new law is also very strict to meet the prisoners in jail
 section 33 (si) ke tahat kisi jiladhikari kii anumati ke baad hi upicoca ke aaropee saathi kaidiyon se mil sakate hai, wo bhi hafte main keval ek se do baar
 There will be a special court for hearing of UPCOCA, the Yogi government wanted to approve this bill only during the winter session, from life imprisonment to death sentence
 lekin isaki kavayad shuru hote hi vipaksh ne is kanoon kaa virodh karnaa shuru kar diya tha
